We compress to 15/30/60 for faster pace.\n16\t\n17\tconst WINDOWS = {\n18\t  BREAKING: 30 * 60 * 1000,     // 30 min: velocity window for breaking\n19\t  RECENT: 15 * 60 * 1000,       // 15 min: very recent activity\n20\t  TRENDING: 60 * 60 * 1000,     // 1 hour: trending growth window\n21\t  MEDIUM: 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000,   // 2 hours: medium-term context\n22\t  FULL: 6 * 60 * 60 * 1000,     // 6 hours: full story window\n23\t};\n24\t\n25\t// ─── Category Decay Curves (ported from TopicPulse) ─────────────────────────\n26\t// Each array = multiplier at 15-min intervals. Higher = more weight at that age.\n27\t// News peaks immediately then decays; sports/entertainment peak later.\n28\t\n29\tconst DECAY_CURVES: Record<string, number[]> = {\n30\t  // News/breaking: peaks immediately, decays fast\n31\t  CRIME:       [100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5, 2, 1],\n32\t  TRAFFIC:     [100, 100, 80, 50, 30, 15, 5, 2, 1],\n33\t  WEATHER:     [100, 100, 100, 80, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5],\n34\t  POLITICS:    [80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n35\t  // Sustained interest: slower decay\n36\t  BUSINESS:    [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n37\t  HEALTH:      [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n38\t  EDUCATION:   [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n39\t  TECHNOLOGY:  [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n40\t  // Entertainment/sports: peaks later, longer tail\n41\t  SPORTS:      [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n42\t  ENTERTAINMENT: [40, 40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 20],\n43\t  COMMUNITY:   [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n44\t  ENVIRONMENT: [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n45\t};\n46\t\n47\tconst DEFAULT_CURVE = [80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5];\n48\t\n49\t/**\n50\t * Get category decay multiplier (0-1) for a story's age.\n51\t * Ported from TopicPulse's story_category_types time_multipliers.\n52\t */\n53\tfunction getCategoryDecay(category: string | null, ageMinutes: number): number {\n54\t  const curve = DECAY_CURVES[category || ''] || DEFAULT_CURVE;\n55\t  const index = Math.floor(ageMinutes / 15); // 15-min intervals\n56\t  if (index >= curve.length) return curve[curve.length - 1] / 100;\n57\t  return curve[index] / 100;\n58\t}\n59\t\n60\t/**\n61\t * Calculate percentage-based growth (ported from TopicPulse Calculator).\n62\t * growth = 100 × (current / past - 1)\n63\t */\n64\tfunction calculateGrowthPercent(current: number, past: number): number {\n65\t  if (past === 0) return current > 0 ? 100 : 0;\n66\t  return 100 * (current / past - 1);\n67\t}\n68\t\n69\t// ─── Score Calculations ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n70\t\n71\t/**\n72\t * Calculate breaking score with compressed time windows for hyperlocal.\n73\t * Uses 30-min velocity (vs TopicPulse's 2h) and 15-min recency.\n74\t */\n75\tasync function calculateBreakingScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n76\t  const thirtyMinAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.BREAKING);\n77\t  const fifteenMinAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.RECENT);\n78\t\n79\t  const recentSources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n80\t    where: {\n81\t      storyId,\n82\t      addedAt: { gte: thirtyMinAgo },\n83\t    },\n84\t    include: {\n85\t      sourcePost: {\n86\t        include: { source: s.addedAt >= fifteenMinAgo).length;\n93\t  const velocityScore = Math.min(1.0, veryRecentCount / 3); // 3 posts in 15 min = max\n94\t\n95\t  // Source diversity: unique sources in 30-min window\n96\t  const uniqueSources = new Set(recentSources.map((ss) => ss.sourcePost.sourceId));\n97\t  const diversityScore = Math.min(1.0, uniqueSources.size / 3); // 3 unique sources = max\n98\t\n99\t  // Recency: exponential decay with 30-min half-life (vs TopicPulse's 2h)\n100\t  const story = await prisma.story.findUnique({ where: { id: storyId } });\n101\t  if (!story) return 0;\n102\t\n103\t  const ageMs = Date.now() - story.lastUpdatedAt.getTime();\n104\t  const ageMinutes = ageMs / (1000 * 60);\n105\t  const halfLifeMinutes = 30;\n106\t  const recencyScore = Math.exp((-Math.LN2 * ageMinutes) / halfLifeMinutes);\n107\t\n108\t  // Category decay multiplier\n109\t  const categoryDecay = getCategoryDecay(story.category, ageMinutes);\n110\t\n111\t  // Weighted combination × category decay\n112\t  const rawScore = 0.40 * velocityScore + 0.30 * diversityScore + 0.30 * recencyScore;\n113\t  const breakingScore = rawScore * categoryDecay;\n114\t\n115\t  return Math.min(1.0, */\n122\tasync function calculateTrendingScore(storyId: string): Promise<{\n123\t  score: number;\n124\t  growthPercent15: number;\n125\t  growthPercent60: number;\n126\t}> {\n127\t  const oneHourAgo });\n138\t\n139\t  // Split into time buckets for growth calculation\n140\t  const last15Min = allSources.filter((s) => s.addedAt >= fifteenMinAgo);\n141\t  const last60Min = allSources.filter((s) => if (older60Min.length > 0) {\n154\t    const growthRate = last60Min.length / older60Min.length;\n155\t    growthScore = Math.min(1.0, growthRate / 2); // 2x growth = max\n156\t  } else if (last60Min.length > 0) {\n157\t    growthScore = 0.5; // New story\n158\t  }\n159\t  // Boost if percentage growth is high (TopicPulse insight)\n160\t  if (growthPercent15 > 50) growthScore = Math.min(1.0, growthScore + 0.2);\n161\t\n162\t  // Engagement\n163\t  const totalEngagement = allSources.reduce((sum, s) => {\n164\t    return sum +\n165\t      s.sourcePost.engagementLikes +\n166\t      s.sourcePost.engagementShares * 2 +\n167\t      s.sourcePost.engagementComments;\n168\t  }, 0);\n169\t  const engagementScore = Math.min(1.0, totalEngagement / 500); // Lower cap for hyperlocal\n170\t\n171\t  // Source count\n172\t  const sourceCountScore = Math.min(1.0, allSources.length / 5); // Lower cap for hyperlocal\n173\t\n174\t  const trendingScore = 0.40 * growthScore + 0.30 * engagementScore + 0.30 * sourceCountScore;\n175\t\n176\t  return {\n177\t    score: Math.min(1.0, Math.max(0, trendingScore)),\n178\t    growthPercent15,\n179\t    growthPercent60,\n180\t  };\n181\t}\n182\t\n183\t/**\n184\t * Calculate confidence score based on source count and trust scores\n185\t */\n186\tasync function calculateConfidenceScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n187\t  const storySources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n188\t    where: { storyId },\n189\t    include: {\n190\t      sourcePost: {\n191\t        include: { source: true },\n192\t      },\n193\t    },\n194\t  });\n195\t\n196\t  if (storySources.length === 0) return 0;\n197\t\n198\t  const sourceCount = storySources.length;\n199\t  const sourceCountFactor = Math.min(1.0, sourceCount / 5);\n200\t\n201\t  const avgTrustScore = storySources.reduce(\n202\t    (sum, ss) => sum + ss.sourcePost.source.trustScore,\n203\t    0\n204\t  ) / storySources.length;\n205\t\n206\t  return sourceCountFactor * avgTrustScore;\n207\t}\n208\t\n209\t/**\n210\t * Calculate locality score based on market-specific mentions\n211\t */\n212\tasync function calculateLocalityScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n213\t  const storySources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n214\t    where: { storyId },\n215\t    include: { sourcePost: true },\n216\t  });\n217\t\n218\t  if (storySources.length === 0) return 0;\n219\t\n220\t  let totalLocalityScore = 0;\n221\t\n222\t  for (const ss of storySources) {\n223\t    const text = `${ss.sourcePost.title || ''} ${ss.sourcePost.content}`;\n224\t    const neighborhoods = detectNeighborhoods(text);\n225\t\n226\t    const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();\n227\t    let postScore = 0;\n228\t\n229\t    if (lowerText.includes('houston') || neighborhoods.length > 0) {\n230\t      postScore = 0.3;\n231\t    }\n232\t\n233\t    if (neighborhoods.length > 0) {\n234\t      postScore += Math.min(0.4, neighborhoods.length * 0.15);\n235\t    }\n236\t\n237\t    const landmarks = [\n238\t      'nrg', 'minute maid', 'toyota center', 'george r. brown',\n239\t      'hermann park', 'discovery green', 'buffalo bayou', 'nasa',\n240\t      'johnson space center', 'port of houston', 'ship channel',\n241\t      'texas medical center', 'rice university', 'university of houston',\n242\t    ];\n243\t\n244\t    for (const landmark of landmarks) {\n245\t      if (lowerText.includes(landmark)) {\n246\t        postScore += 0.1;\n247\t      }\n248\t    }\n249\t\n250\t    totalLocalityScore += Math.min(1.0, postScore);\n251\t  }\n252\t\n253\t  return Math.min(1.0, totalLocalityScore / storySources.length);\n254\t}\n255\t\n256\t// ─── Status Determination (ported from TopicPulse's tiered logic) ───────────\n257\t\n258\t/**\n259\t * Ported from TopicPulse's level_stay_hot_default.\n260\t * Breaking stories get a minimum retention period before they can decay.\n261\t */\n262\tfunction shouldRetainBreaking(\n263\t  breakingScore: number,\n264\t  minutesInBreaking: number,\n265\t  growthPercent15: number,\n266\t): boolean {\n267\t  // Minimum 15 minutes at breaking (TopicPulse: 2h; we compress to 15min)\n268\t  if (minutesInBreaking <= 15) return true;\n269\t\n270\t  // Up to 2 hours: stay breaking if 15-min growth > 20%\n271\t  if (minutesInBreaking <= 120 && growthPercent15 > 20) return true;\n272\t\n273\t  // Stay breaking if score still above threshold\n274\t  if (breakingScore > 0.6) return true;\n275\t\n276\t  return false;\n277\t}\n278\t\n279\t/**\n280\t * Determine story status using TopicPulse-inspired tiered logic.\n281\t *\n282\t * Tier 1 (< 15 min): Absolute score thresholds\n283\t * Tier 2 (15-60 min): Growth + score hybrid\n284\t * Tier 3 (> 60 min): Growth-dominant with explicit decay\n285\t */\n286\tfunction determineStatus(\n287\t  currentStatus: string,\n288\t  breakingScore: number,\n289\t  trendingScore: number,\n290\t  growthPercent15: number,\n291\t  growthPercent60: number,\n292\t  ageMinutes: number,\n293\t  lastStatusChangeMinutes: number,\n294\t): string {\n295\t  // ── Tier 1: Very fresh (< 15 minutes) ──\n296\t  if (ageMinutes < 15) {\n297\t    if (breakingScore > 0.6) return 'BREAKING';\n298\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4 || breakingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n299\t    return 'EMERGING';\n300\t  }\n301\t\n302\t  // ── Tier 2: Developing (15-60 minutes) ──\n303\t  if (ageMinutes < 60) {\n304\t    // Breaking: high score OR (moderate score + rapid growth)\n305\t    if (breakingScore > 0.7) return 'BREAKING';\n306\t    if (breakingScore > 0.5 && growthPercent15 > 30) return 'BREAKING';\n307\t\n308\t    // Breaking retention (ported from TopicPulse level_stay_hot)\n309\t    if (currentStatus === 'BREAKING') {\n310\t      if (shouldRetainBreaking(breakingScore, lastStatusChangeMinutes, growthPercent15)) {\n311\t        return 'BREAKING';\n312\t      }\n313\t      return 'TRENDING'; // Graceful decay to trending\n314\t    }\n315\t\n316\t    // Trending: sustained growth or high score\n317\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n318\t    if (growthPercent15 > 50) return 'TRENDING'; // Rapid growth alone triggers trending\n319\t\n320\t    return 'EMERGING';\n321\t  }\n322\t\n323\t  // ── Tier 3: Maturing (> 60 minutes) ──\n324\t\n325\t  // Breaking with retention check\n326\t  if (breakingScore > 0.7) return 'BREAKING';\n327\t  if (currentStatus === 'BREAKING') {\n328\t    if (shouldRetainBreaking(breakingScore, lastStatusChangeMinutes, growthPercent15)) {\n329\t      return 'BREAKING';\n330\t    }\n331\t    return 'TRENDING';\n332\t  }\n333\t\n334\t  // Trending: needs growth to stay trending (ported from TopicPulse tier3)\n335\t  if (currentStatus === 'TRENDING') {\n336\t    // TopicPulse: decay if 90-min growth < 8%. We use 60-min growth < 10%.\n337\t    if (growthPercent60 < 10 && lastStatusChangeMinutes > 60) {\n338\t      return 'ACTIVE'; // Explicit decay: trending → active\n339\t    }\n340\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n341\t    return 'ACTIVE';\n342\t  }\n343\t\n344\t  // New trending detection\n345\t  if (trendingScore > 0.5) return 'TRENDING';\n346\t  if (growthPercent15 > 50 && trendingScore > 0.3) return 'TRENDING';\n347\t\n348\t  // Age-based decay (ported from TopicPulse flat→stop→dead)\n349\t  if (ageMinutes > 48 * 60) return 'STALE';\n350\t  if (ageMinutes > 12 * 60) return 'ACTIVE';\n351\t  if (ageMinutes > 3 * 60) {\n352\t    // After 3 hours at ACTIVE with no growth → STALE\n353\t    if (currentStatus === 'ACTIVE' && lastStatusChangeMinutes > 180 && growthPercent60 < 5) {\n354\t      return 'STALE';\n355\t    }\n356\t    return 'ACTIVE';\n357\t  }\n358\t\n359\t  return currentStatus === 'EMERGING' ? 'EMERGING' : 'ACTIVE';\n360\t}\n361\t\n362\t// ─── Main Processing ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n363\t\n364\tasync function processScoring(job: Job<ScoringJob>): Promise<void> {\n365\t  const { storyId } = job.data;\n366\t\n367\t  logger.info({ storyId }, 'Scoring story');\n368\t\n369\t  const story = await prisma.story.findUnique({\n370\t    where: { id: storyId },\n371\t  });\n372\t\n373\t  if (!story) {\n374\t    logger.warn({ storyId }, 'Story not found, skipping scoring');\n375\t    return;\n376\t  }\n377\t\n378\t  // Calculate all scores\n379\t  const [breakingScore, trendingResult, confidenceScore, localityScore] = await Promise.all([\n380\t    calculateBreakingScore(storyId),\n381\t    calculateTrendingScore(storyId),\n382\t    calculateConfidenceScore(storyId),\n383\t    calculateLocalityScore(storyId),\n384\t  ]);\n385\t\n386\t  const trendingScore = trendingResult.score;\n387\t\n388\t  // Composite score\n389\t  const compositeScore =\n390\t    0.35 * breakingScore +\n391\t    0.25 * trendingScore +\n392\t    0.20 * confidenceScore +\n393\t    0.20 * localityScore;\n394\t\n395\t  // Determine status with tiered logic\n396\t  const ageMs = Date.now() - story.firstSeenAt.getTime();\n397\t  const ageMinutes = ageMs / (1000 * 60);\n398\t  const previousStatus = story.status;\n399\t\n400\t  // Time since last status change (for retention/decay logic)\n401\t  const lastStatusChangeMs = story.lastUpdatedAt\n402\t    ? Date.now() - story.lastUpdatedAt.getTime()\n403\t    : ageMs;\n404\t  const lastStatusChangeMinutes = lastStatusChangeMs / (1000 * 60);\n405\t\n406\t  const newStatus = determineStatus(\n407\t    previousStatus,\n408\t    breakingScore,\n409\t    trendingScore,\n410\t    trendingResult.growthPercent15,\n411\t    trendingResult.growthPercent60,\n412\t    ageMinutes,\n413\t    lastStatusChangeMinutes,\n414\t  );\n415\t\n416\t  // Update story with scores\n417\t  await prisma.story.update({\n418\t    where: { id: storyId },\n419\t    data: {\n420\t      breakingScore,\n421\t      trendingScore,\n422\t      confidenceScore,\n423\t      localityScore,\n424\t      compositeScore,\n425\t      status: newStatus as 'EMERGING' | 'BREAKING' | 'TRENDING' | 'ACTIVE' | 'STALE' | 'ARCHIVED',\n426\t    },\n427\t  });\n428\t\n429\t  // Create score snapshot\n430\t  await prisma.scoreSnapshot.create({\n431\t    data: {\n432\t      storyId,\n433\t      breakingScore,\n434\t      trendingScore,\n435\t      confidenceScore,\n436\t      localityScore,\n437\t      compositeScore,\n438\t    },\n439\t  });\n440\t\n441\t  // Log status changes\n442\t  if (previousStatus !== newStatus) {\n443\t    logger.info({\n444\t      storyId,\n445\t      previousStatus,\n446\t      newStatus,\n447\t      breakingScore,\n448\t      trendingScore,\n449\t      growthPercent15: trendingResult.growthPercent15.toFixed(1),\n450\t      growthPercent60: trendingResult.growthPercent60.toFixed(1),\n451\t      ageMinutes: Math.round(ageMinutes),\n452\t    }, 'Story status changed');\n453\t  }\n454\t\n455\t  logger.info({\n456\t    storyId,\n457\t    breakingScore: breakingScore.toFixed(3),\n458\t    trendingScore: trendingScore.toFixed(3),\n459\t    confidenceScore: confidenceScore.toFixed(3),\n460\t    localityScore: localityScore.toFixed(3),\n461\t    compositeScore: compositeScore.toFixed(3),\n462\t    status: newStatus,\n463\t  }, 'Scoring complete');\n464\t}\n465\t\n466\texport function createScoringWorker(): Worker {\n467\t  const connection = getSharedConnection();\n468\t\n469\t  const worker = new Worker<ScoringJob>(\n470\t    'scoring',\n471\t    async (job) => {\n472\t      await processScoring(job);\n473\t    },\n474\t    {\n475\t      connection,\n476\t      concurrency: 5,\n477\t    }\n478\t  );\n479\t\n480\t  worker.on('completed', (job) => {\n481\t    logger.info({ jobId: job.id }, 'Scoring job completed');\n482\t  });\n483\t\n484\t  worker.on('failed', (job, err) => {\n485\t    logger.error({ jobId: job?.id, err: err.message }, 'Scoring job failed');\n486\t  });\n487\t\n488\t  return worker;\n489\t}\n490\t"}]},"uuid":"1efedd2f-94df-4a2f-9492-f341087b46ed","timestamp":"2026-03-30T03:06:11.617Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"898bfd43-bad5-4ba2-b467-25972d6a3256","userType":"external","entrypoint":"remote","cwd":"/home/user/TPHyperlocal","sessionId":"718d6e94-39e0-4383-806d-19278e92a3b9","version":"2.1.87","gitBranch":"main","slug":"goofy-sprouting-sprout"}

RSSItem): string[] {\n88\t  const urls: string[] = [];\n89\t  if (item['media:content']) {\n90\t    const media = Array.isArray(item['media:content'])\n91\t      ? item['media:content']\n92\t      : where: { platformPostId },\n155\t      });\n156\t      if (existing) continue;\n157\t\n158\t      const contentHash = generateContentHash(`${title} ${content}`);\n159\t      const publishedAt = Retry after ${delay}ms`);\n321\t  }\n322\t\n323\t  if (!response.ok) {\n324\t    const body = await response.text();\n325\t    throw new Error(`Facebook API error: ${response.status} - ${body}`);\n326\t  }\n327\t\n328\t  const data = (await response.json()) as { data: FacebookPost[] };\n329\t\n330\t  const enrichmentQueue = new Queue('enrichment', {\n331\t    connection: getSharedConnection(),\n332\t  });\n333\t\n334\t  let ingested = 0;\n335\t\n336\t  for (const fbPost of data.data) {\n337\t    try {\n338\t      const content = fbPost.message || fbPost.story || '';\n339\t      if (!content) continue; // Skip posts with no text content\n340\t\n341\t      const platformPostId = `facebook::${fbPost.id}`;\n342\t\n343\t      const existing = await prisma.sourcePost.findUnique({\n344\t        where: { platformPostId },\n345\t      });\n346\t      if (existing) continue;\n347\t\n348\t      const contentHash = generateContentHash(content);\n349\t      const mediaUrls = fbPost.full_picture ? ingested++;\n368\t\n369\t      await enrichmentQueue.add('enrich', { sourcePostId: post.id }, {\n370\t        attempts: 3,\n371\t        backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 2000 },\n372\t 'Facebook poll complete');\n386\t}\n387\t\n388\texport function createIngestionWorker(): Worker {\n389\t  const connection = getSharedConnection();\n390\t\n391\t  const worker = new Worker<IngestionJob>(\n392\t    'ingestion',\n393\t    async (job: Job<IngestionJob>) => {\n394\t      logger.info({ jobId: job.id, type: job.data.type }, 'Processing ingestion job');\n395\t\n396\t      switch (job.data.type) {\n397\t        case 'rss_poll':\n398\t          await handleRSSPoll(job as Job<RSSPollJob>);\n399\t          break;\n400\t        case 'newsapi_poll':\n401\t          await }\n537\t}\n538\t\n539\t/**\n540\t * Schedule digest email jobs for subscriptions that are due\n541\t */\n542\tasync function scheduleDigests(): Promise<void> {\n543\t  const { digestQueue } = getQueues();\n544\t\n545\t  try {\n546\t    const now = new Date();\n547\t\n548\t    const subscriptions = await prisma.digestSubscription.findMany({\n549\t      where: {\n550\t        isActive: true,\n551\t      },\n552\t    });\n553\t\n554\t    // Filter to only subscriptions that are due based on frequency and lastSentAt\n555\t    const dueSubscriptions = subscriptions.filter((sub) => {\n556\t      if (!sub.lastSentAt) return true; // Never sent, so it's due\n557\t\n558\t      const lastSent = sub.lastSentAt.getTime();\n559\t      const elapsed = now.getTime() - lastSent;\n560\t\n561\t      switch (sub.frequency) {\n562\t        case 'HOURLY':\n563\t          return elapsed >= 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 hour\n564\t        case 'TWICE_DAILY':\n565\t          return elapsed >= 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 12 hours\n566\t        case 'DAILY':\n567\t          return elapsed >= 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours\n568\t        case 'WEEKLY':\n569\t          return elapsed >= 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 7 days\n570\t        default:\n571\t          return false;\n572\t      }\n573\t    });\n574\t\n575\t    logger.info({ count: dueSubscriptions.length, total: subscriptions.length }, 'Scheduling digest jobs');\n576\t\n577\t    for (const sub of dueSubscriptions) {\n578\t      await digestQueue.add(\n579\t        'send_digest',\n580\t        {\n581\t          type: 'send_digest',\n582\t          subscriptionId: sub.id,\n583\t          accountId: sub.accountId,\n584\t          userId: sub.userId,\n585\t          email: sub.email,\n586\t          frequency: sub.frequency,\n587\t          timezone: sub.timezone,\n588\t          filters: sub.filters,\n589\t        },\n590\t        {\n591\t          jobId: `digest-${sub.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n592\t          attempts: 3,\n593\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 10000 },\n594\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n595\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n596\t        }\n597\t      );\n598\t    }\n599\t  } catch (err) {\n600\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule digests');\n601\t  }\n602\t}\n603\t\n604\t/**\n605\t * Re-score all non-archived stories to apply score .default('compositeScore'),\n23\t  order: z.enum(['asc', 'desc']).default('desc'),\n24\t});\n25\t\n26\tconst StoryIdParamsSchema = z.object({\n27\t  id: z.string().min(1),\n28\t});\n29\t\n30\texport async function storiesRoutes(\n31\t  app: FastifyInstance,\n32\t  _opts: FastifyPluginOptions,\n33\t) {\n34\t  // GET /api/v1/stories - list stories with filtering and pagination\n35\t  app.get('/stories', async (request, reply) => {\n36\t    const parseResult = ListStoriesQuerySchema.safeParse(request.query);\n37\t    if (!parseResult.success) {\n38\t      return reply.status(400).send({\n39\t        error: 'Invalid query parameters',\n40\t        details: parseResult.error.flatten().fieldErrors,\n41\t      });\n42\t    }\n43\t\n44\t    const { status, category, sourceIds, minScore, maxAge, limit, offset, sort, order } =\n45\t      parseResult.data;\n46\t\n47\t    const where: Prisma.StoryWhereInput = {\n48\t      mergedIntoId: null, // exclude merged stories\n49\t    };\n50\t\n51\t    if (status) {\n52\t      const statuses = status.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n53\t      if (statuses.length === 1) {\n54\t        where.status = statuses[0] as StoryStatus;\n55\t      } else if (statuses.length > 1) {\n56\t        where.status = { in: statuses as StoryStatus[] };\n57\t      }\n58\t    }\n59\t\n60\t    if (category) {\n61\t      const categories = category.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n62\t      const hasUnknown = categories.includes('Unknown');\n63\t      const named = categories.filter((c) => c !== 'Unknown');\n64\t\n65\t      if (hasUnknown && named.length > 0) {\n66\t        where.OR = [\n67\t          { category: { in: named } },\n68\t          { category: null },\n69\t        ];\n70\t      } else if (hasUnknown) {\n71\t        where.category = null;\n72\t      } else if (named.length === 1) {\n73\t        where.category = named[0];\n74\t      } else if (named.length > 1) {\n75\t        where.category = { in: named };\n76\t      }\n77\t    }\n78\t\n79\t    if (sourceIds) {\n80\t      const ids = sourceIds.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n81\t      if (ids.length > 0) {\n82\t        where.storySources = {\n83\t          some: {\n84\t            sourcePost: {\n85\t              sourceId: { in: ids },\n86\t            },\n87\t          },\n88\t        };\n89\t      }\n90\t    }\n91\t\n92\t    if (minScore !== undefined) {\n93\t      where.compositeScore = { gte: minScore };\n94\t    }\n95\t\n96\t    if (maxAge !== undefined) {\n97\t      const cutoff = new Date(Date.now() - maxAge * 60 * 60 * 1000);\n98\t      where.firstSeenAt = { gte: cutoff };\n99\t    }\n100\t\n101\t    // Build facet where clauses — each facet excludes its own filter\n102\t    // so counts show what's available if you change that filter\n103\t    const baseFacetWhere: Prisma.StoryWhereInput = { mergedIntoId: null };\n104\t    if (maxAge !== undefined) {\n105\t      baseFacetWhere.firstSeenAt = { gte: new Date(Date.now() - maxAge * 60 * 60 * 1000) };\n106\t    }\n107\t    if (minScore !== undefined) {\n108\t      baseFacetWhere.compositeScore = { gte: minScore };\n109\t    }\n110\t    if (sourceIds) {\n111\t      const ids = sourceIds.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n112\t      if (ids.length > 0) {\n113\t        baseFacetWhere.storySources = { some: { sourcePost: { sourceId: { in: ids } } } };\n114\t      }\n115\t    }\n116\t\n117\t    // Category facet where: includes status + source filters, excludes category\n118\t    const catFacetWhere: Prisma.StoryWhereInput = { ...baseFacetWhere };\n119\t    if (status) {\n120\t      const statuses = status.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n121\t      catFacetWhere.status = statuses.length === 1\n122\t        ? (statuses[0] as StoryStatus)\n123\t        : { in: statuses as StoryStatus[] };\n124\t    }\n125\t\n126\t    // Helper: apply category filter to a where clause (handles Unknown → null)\n127\t    function applyCategoryFilter(w: Prisma.StoryWhereInput) {\n128\t      if (!category) return;\n129\t      const cats = category.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n130\t      const hasUnknown = cats.includes('Unknown');\n131\t      const named = cats.filter((c) => c !== 'Unknown');\n132\t      if (hasUnknown && named.length > 0) {\n133\t        w.OR = [...(w.OR || []), { category: { in: named } }, { category: null }];\n134\t      } else if (hasUnknown) {\n135\t        w.category = null;\n136\t      } else if (named.length === 1) {\n137\t        w.category = named[0];\n138\t      } else if (named.length > 1) {\n139\t        w.category = { in: named };\n140\t      }\n141\t    }\n142\t\n143\t    // Status facet where: includes category + source filters, excludes status\n144\t    const statusFacetWhere: Prisma.StoryWhereInput = { ...baseFacetWhere };\n145\t    applyCategoryFilter(statusFacetWhere);\n146\t\n147\t    // Source facet where: includes status + category filters, excludes source\n148\t    const sourceFacetWhere: Prisma.StoryWhereInput = { ...baseFacetWhere };\n149\t    if (status) {\n150\t      const statuses = status.split(',').map((s) => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n151\t      sourceFacetWhere.status = statuses.length === 1\n152\t        ? name: string; platform: string; count: bigint }>>`\n201\t        SELECT s.id, s.name, s.platform, COUNT(DISTINCT st.id)::bigint as count\n202\t        FROM \"Source\" s\n203\t        JOIN \"SourcePost\" sp ON sp.\"sourceId\" = s.id\n204\t        JOIN \"StorySource\" ss ON ss.\"sourcePostId\" = sp.id\n205\t        JOIN \"Story\" st ON st.id = ss.\"storyId\"\n206\t        WHERE s.\"isActive\" = true\n207\t          AND st.\"mergedIntoId\" IS NULL\n208\t          ${maxAge !== undefined ? Prisma.sql`AND st.\"firstSeenAt\" >= ${new Date(Date.now() - maxAge * 60 * 60 * 1000)}` : Prisma.empty}\n209\t          ${minScore !== undefined ? Prisma.sql`AND st.\"compositeScore\" >= ${minScore}` : Prisma.empty}\n210\t          ${status ? Prisma.sql`AND st.status IN (${Prisma.join(status.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean))})` : Prisma.empty}\n211\t          ${category ? (() => {\n212\t            const cats = category.split(',').map(s => s.trim()).filter(Boolean);\n213\t            const hasUnknown = cats.includes('Unknown');\n214\t            const named = cats.filter(c => c !== 'Unknown');\n215\t            if (hasUnknown && named.length > 0) {\n216\t              return Prisma.sql`AND (st.category IN (${Prisma.join(named)}) OR st.category IS NULL)`;\n217\t            } else if (hasUnknown) {\n218\t              return Prisma.sql`AND st.category IS NULL`;\n219\t            } else {\n220\t              return Prisma.sql`AND st.category IN (${Prisma.join(named)})`;\n221\t            }\n222\t          })() : Prisma.empty}\n223\t        GROUP BY s.id, s.name, s.platform\n224\t        ORDER BY count DESC\n225\t      `,\n226\t    ]);\n227\t\n228\t    return reply.send({\n229\t      data: stories,\n230\t      pagination: {\n231\t        total,\n232\t        limit,\n233\t        offset,\n234\t        hasMore: offset + limit < total,\n235\t      },\n236\t      facets: {\n237\t        categories: categoryFacets.map((r) => ({\n238\t          name: r.category || 'Unknown',\n239\t          count: r._count._all,\n240\t        })),\n241\t        statuses: statusFacets.map((r) => ({\n242\t          name: r.status,\n243\t          count: r._count._all,\n244\t        })),\n245\t        sources: sourceData.map((r) => ({\n246\t          id: r.id,\n247\t          name: r.name,\n248\t          platform: r.platform,\n249\t          storyCount: Number(r.count),\n250\t        })),\n251\t      },\n252\t    });\n253\t  });\n254\t\n255\t  // GET /api/v1/stories/sources - $last_story)\n271\t\t{\n272\t\t\t$retrospective_minutes = intval($this->algorithm['tier3_retrospective_minutes']);\n273\t\t\tif(empty($retrospective_minutes))\n274\t\t\t{\n275\t\t\t\t$retrospective_minutes = 45;\n276\t\t\t}\n277\t\n278\t\t\t$change = $last_story)\n327\t\t{\n328\t\t\tif($story['score'] >= 165) return $this->levels['hot'];\n329\t\n330\t\t\tif($story['score'] >= 85) return $this->levels['trending'];\n331\t\n332\t\t\treturn    }\n313\t\n314\t    /**\n315\t     * Marks a group as private.\n316\t     *\n317\t     * @param $crGroupId\n318\t     */\n319\t    private function markUrlPrivate($crGroupId)\n320\t    {\n321\t It can be either false if the URL is not valid or a valid reader\n388\t     *   if the URL has a supported reader.\n389\t     */\n390\t    protected function getValidUrlDetails($url)\n391\t    {\n392\t        $returnDetails = [\n393\t            'url' => $url,\n394\t            'reader' => false,\n395\t        ];\n396\t\n397\t        if (!$this->isValidHttpsUrl($url)) {\n398\t $returnDetails['error'] = 'URL not supported';\n413\t        return $returnDetails;\n414\t    }\n415\t\n416\t    /**\n417\t     * Checks if a given URL is a valid HTTPS URL.\n418\t     *\n419\t     *    {\n424\t        $urlDetails = parse_url($url);\n425\t        if (empty($urlDetails['scheme']) || $urlDetails['scheme'] !== 'https') {\n426\t            return false;\n427\t        }\n428\t        if (!empty($urlDetails['port']) && $urlDetails['port'] !== 443) {\n429\t            return false;\n430\t        }\n431\t        return true;\n432\t    }\n433\t\n434\t    /**\n435\t     * Validates a Facebook Group URL, or false otherwise.\n440\t     */\n441\t    protected function validateFacebookGroupUrl($url)\n442\t    {\n443\t        $urlDetails = parse_url($url);\n444\t        if (strpos($urlDetails['host'], 'facebook.com') === false) {\n445\t            return false;\n446\t        }\n447\t        if (strpos($urlDetails['path'], '/groups/') !== 0) {\n448\t            return false;\n449\t        }\n450\t//        $urlDetails['host'] = 'www.facebook.com';\n451\t        return \"{$urlDetails['scheme']}://{$urlDetails['host']}{$urlDetails['path']}\";\n452\t We compress to 15/30/60 for faster pace.\n16\t\n17\tconst WINDOWS = {\n18\t  BREAKING: 30 * 60 * 1000,     // 30 min: velocity window for breaking\n19\t  RECENT: 15 * 60 * 1000,       // 15 min: very recent activity\n20\t  TRENDING: 60 * 60 * 1000,     // 1 hour: trending growth window\n21\t  MEDIUM: 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000,   // 2 hours: medium-term context\n22\t  FULL: 6 * 60 * 60 * 1000,     // 6 hours: full story window\n23\t};\n24\t\n25\t// ─── Category Decay Curves (ported from TopicPulse) ─────────────────────────\n26\t// Each array = multiplier at 15-min intervals. Higher = more weight at that age.\n27\t// News peaks immediately then decays; sports/entertainment peak later.\n28\t\n29\tconst DECAY_CURVES: Record<string, number[]> = {\n30\t  // News/breaking: peaks immediately, decays fast\n31\t  CRIME:       [100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5, 2, 1],\n32\t  TRAFFIC:     [100, 100, 80, 50, 30, 15, 5, 2, 1],\n33\t  WEATHER:     [100, 100, 100, 80, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5],\n34\t  POLITICS:    [80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n35\t  // Sustained interest: slower decay\n36\t  BUSINESS:    [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n37\t  HEALTH:      [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20, 10],\n38\t  EDUCATION:   [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n39\t  TECHNOLOGY:  [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n40\t  // Entertainment/sports: peaks later, longer tail\n41\t  SPORTS:      [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n42\t  ENTERTAINMENT: [40, 40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 20],\n43\t  COMMUNITY:   [60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n44\t  ENVIRONMENT: [40, 60, 80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 50, 40, 30, 20],\n45\t};\n46\t\n47\tconst DEFAULT_CURVE = [80, 100, 100, 80, 60, 40, 30, 20, 10, 5];\n48\t\n49\t/**\n50\t * Get category decay multiplier (0-1) for a story's age.\n51\t * Ported from TopicPulse's story_category_types time_multipliers.\n52\t */\n53\tfunction getCategoryDecay(category: string | null, ageMinutes: number): number {\n54\t  const curve = DECAY_CURVES[category || ''] || DEFAULT_CURVE;\n55\t  const index = Math.floor(ageMinutes / 15); // 15-min intervals\n56\t  if (index >= curve.length) return curve[curve.length - 1] / 100;\n57\t  return curve[index] / 100;\n58\t}\n59\t\n60\t/**\n61\t * Calculate percentage-based growth (ported from TopicPulse Calculator).\n62\t * growth = 100 × (current / past - 1)\n63\t */\n64\tfunction calculateGrowthPercent(current: number, past: number): number {\n65\t  if (past === 0) return current > 0 ? 100 : 0;\n66\t  return 100 * (current / past - 1);\n67\t}\n68\t\n69\t// ─── Score Calculations ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n70\t\n71\t/**\n72\t * Calculate breaking score with compressed time windows for hyperlocal.\n73\t * Uses 30-min velocity (vs TopicPulse's 2h) and 15-min recency.\n74\t */\n75\tasync function calculateBreakingScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n76\t  const thirtyMinAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.BREAKING);\n77\t  const fifteenMinAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.RECENT);\n78\t\n79\t  const recentSources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n80\t    where: {\n81\t      storyId,\n82\t      addedAt: { gte: thirtyMinAgo },\n83\t    },\n84\t    include: {\n85\t      sourcePost: {\n86\t        include: { source: true },\n87\t      },\n88\t    },\n89\t  });\n90\t\n91\t  // Velocity: posts per 15 min in last 30 min (more sensitive than per hour)\n92\t  const veryRecentCount = recentSources.filter((s) => s.addedAt >= fifteenMinAgo).length;\n93\t  const velocityScore = Math.min(1.0, veryRecentCount / 3); // 3 posts in 15 min = max\n94\t\n95\t  // Source diversity: unique sources in 30-min window\n96\t  const uniqueSources = new Set(recentSources.map((ss) => ss.sourcePost.sourceId));\n97\t  const diversityScore = Math.min(1.0, uniqueSources.size / 3); // 3 unique sources = max\n98\t\n99\t  // Recency: exponential decay with 30-min half-life (vs TopicPulse's 2h)\n100\t  const story = await prisma.story.findUnique({ where: { id: storyId } });\n101\t  if (!story) return 0;\n102\t\n103\t  const ageMs = Date.now() - story.lastUpdatedAt.getTime();\n104\t  const ageMinutes = ageMs / (1000 * 60);\n105\t  const halfLifeMinutes = 30;\n106\t  const recencyScore = Math.exp((-Math.LN2 * ageMinutes) / halfLifeMinutes);\n107\t\n108\t  // Category decay multiplier\n109\t  const categoryDecay = getCategoryDecay(story.category, ageMinutes);\n110\t\n111\t  // Weighted combination × category decay\n112\t  const rawScore = 0.40 * velocityScore + 0.30 * diversityScore + 0.30 * recencyScore;\n113\t  const breakingScore = rawScore * categoryDecay;\n114\t\n115\t  return Math.min(1.0, Math.max(0, breakingScore));\n116\t}\n117\t\n118\t/**\n119\t * Calculate trending score with growth-percentage tracking\n120\t * (ported from TopicPulse's get_percentages_default).\n121\t */\n122\tasync function calculateTrendingScore(storyId: string): Promise<{\n123\t  score: number;\n124\t  growthPercent15: number;\n125\t  growthPercent60: number;\n126\t}> {\n127\t  const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.TRENDING);\n128\t  const fifteenMinAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.RECENT);\n129\t  const sixHoursAgo = new Date(Date.now() - WINDOWS.FULL);\n130\t\n131\t  const });\n138\t\n139\t  // Split into time buckets for growth calculation\n140\t  const last15Min = allSources.filter((s) => s.addedAt >= fifteenMinAgo);\n141\t  const last60Min = allSources.filter((s) => growthPercent60 = calculateGrowthPercent(last60Min.length, older60Min.length);\n150\t\n151\t  // Growth score: hybrid of ratio and percentage (best of both worlds)\n152\t  let growthScore = 0;\n153\t  if (older60Min.length > 0) {\n154\t    const growthRate = last60Min.length / older60Min.length;\n155\t    growthScore = Math.min(1.0, growthRate / 2); // 2x growth = max\n156\t  } else if (last60Min.length > 0) {\n157\t    growthScore = 0.5; // New story\n158\t  }\n159\t  // Boost if percentage growth is high (TopicPulse insight)\n160\t  if (growthPercent15 > 50) growthScore = Math.min(1.0, growthScore + 0.2);\n161\t\n162\t  // Engagement\n163\t  const totalEngagement = allSources.reduce((sum, s) => {\n164\t    return sum +\n165\t      s.sourcePost.engagementLikes +\n166\t      s.sourcePost.engagementShares * 2 +\n167\t      s.sourcePost.engagementComments;\n168\t  }, 0);\n169\t  const engagementScore = Math.min(1.0, totalEngagement / 500); // Lower cap for hyperlocal\n170\t\n171\t  // Source count\n172\t  const sourceCountScore = Math.min(1.0, allSources.length / 5); // Lower cap for hyperlocal\n173\t\n174\t  const trendingScore = 0.40 * growthScore + 0.30 * engagementScore + 0.30 * sourceCountScore;\n175\t\n176\t  return {\n177\t    score: Math.min(1.0, Math.max(0, trendingScore)),\n178\t    growthPercent15,\n179\t    growthPercent60,\n180\t  };\n181\t}\n182\t\n183\t/**\n184\t * Calculate confidence score based on source count and trust scores\n185\t */\n186\tasync function calculateConfidenceScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n187\t  const storySources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n188\t    where: { storyId },\n189\t    include: {\n190\t      sourcePost: {\n191\t        include: { source: true },\n192\t      },\n193\t    },\n194\t  });\n195\t\n196\t  if (storySources.length === 0) return 0;\n197\t\n198\t  const sourceCount = storySources.length;\n199\t  const sourceCountFactor = Math.min(1.0, sourceCount / 5);\n200\t\n201\t  const avgTrustScore = storySources.reduce(\n202\t    (sum, ss) => sum + ss.sourcePost.source.trustScore,\n203\t    0\n204\t  ) / storySources.length;\n205\t\n206\t  return sourceCountFactor * avgTrustScore;\n207\t}\n208\t\n209\t/**\n210\t * Calculate locality score based on market-specific mentions\n211\t */\n212\tasync function calculateLocalityScore(storyId: string): Promise<number> {\n213\t  const storySources = await prisma.storySource.findMany({\n214\t    where: { storyId },\n215\t    include: { sourcePost: true },\n216\t  });\n217\t\n218\t  if (storySources.length === 0) return 0;\n219\t\n220\t  let totalLocalityScore = 0;\n221\t\n222\t  for (const ss of storySources) {\n223\t    const text = `${ss.sourcePost.title || ''} ${ss.sourcePost.content}`;\n224\t    const neighborhoods = detectNeighborhoods(text);\n225\t\n226\t    const lowerText = text.toLowerCase();\n227\t    let postScore = 0;\n228\t\n229\t    if (lowerText.includes('houston') || neighborhoods.length > 0) {\n230\t      postScore = 0.3;\n231\t    }\n232\t\n233\t    if (neighborhoods.length > 0) {\n234\t      postScore += Math.min(0.4, neighborhoods.length * 0.15);\n235\t    }\n236\t\n237\t    const landmarks = [\n238\t      'nrg', 'minute maid', 'toyota center', 'george r. brown',\n239\t      'hermann park', 'discovery green', 'buffalo bayou', 'nasa',\n240\t      'johnson space center', 'port of houston', 'ship channel',\n241\t      'texas medical center', 'rice university', 'university of houston',\n242\t    ];\n243\t\n244\t    for (const landmark of landmarks) {\n245\t      if (lowerText.includes(landmark)) {\n246\t        postScore += 0.1;\n247\t      }\n248\t    }\n249\t\n250\t    totalLocalityScore += Math.min(1.0, postScore);\n251\t  }\n252\t\n253\t  return Math.min(1.0, totalLocalityScore / storySources.length);\n254\t}\n255\t\n256\t// ─── Status Determination (ported from TopicPulse's tiered logic) ───────────\n257\t\n258\t/**\n259\t * Ported from TopicPulse's level_stay_hot_default.\n260\t * Breaking stories get a minimum retention period before they can decay.\n261\t */\n262\tfunction shouldRetainBreaking(\n263\t  breakingScore: number,\n264\t  minutesInBreaking: number,\n265\t  growthPercent15: number,\n266\t): boolean {\n267\t  // Minimum 15 minutes at breaking (TopicPulse: 2h; we compress to 15min)\n268\t  if (minutesInBreaking <= 15) return true;\n269\t\n270\t  // Up to 2 hours: stay breaking if 15-min growth > 20%\n271\t  if (minutesInBreaking <= 120 && growthPercent15 > 20) return true;\n272\t\n273\t  // Stay breaking if score still above threshold\n274\t  if (breakingScore > 0.6) return true;\n275\t\n276\t  return false;\n277\t}\n278\t\n279\t/**\n280\t * Determine story status using TopicPulse-inspired tiered logic.\n281\t *\n282\t * Tier 1 (< 15 min): Absolute score thresholds\n283\t * Tier 2 (15-60 min): Growth + score hybrid\n284\t * Tier 3 (> 60 min): Growth-dominant with explicit decay\n285\t */\n286\tfunction determineStatus(\n287\t  currentStatus: string,\n288\t  breakingScore: number,\n289\t  trendingScore: number,\n290\t  growthPercent15: number,\n291\t  growthPercent60: number,\n292\t  ageMinutes: number,\n293\t  lastStatusChangeMinutes: number,\n294\t): string {\n295\t  // ── Tier 1: Very fresh (< 15 minutes) ──\n296\t  if (ageMinutes < 15) {\n297\t    if (breakingScore > 0.6) return 'BREAKING';\n298\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4 || breakingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n299\t    return 'EMERGING';\n300\t  }\n301\t\n302\t  // ── Tier 2: Developing (15-60 minutes) ──\n303\t  if (ageMinutes < 60) {\n304\t    // Breaking: high score OR (moderate score + rapid growth)\n305\t    if (breakingScore > 0.7) return 'BREAKING';\n306\t    if (breakingScore > 0.5 && growthPercent15 > 30) return 'BREAKING';\n307\t\n308\t    // Breaking retention (ported from TopicPulse level_stay_hot)\n309\t    if (currentStatus === 'BREAKING') {\n310\t      if (shouldRetainBreaking(breakingScore, lastStatusChangeMinutes, growthPercent15)) {\n311\t        return 'BREAKING';\n312\t      }\n313\t      return 'TRENDING'; // Graceful decay to trending\n314\t    }\n315\t\n316\t    // Trending: sustained growth or high score\n317\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n318\t    if (growthPercent15 > 50) return 'TRENDING'; // Rapid growth alone triggers trending\n319\t\n320\t    return 'EMERGING';\n321\t  }\n322\t\n323\t  // ── Tier 3: Maturing (> 60 minutes) ──\n324\t\n325\t  // Breaking with retention check\n326\t  if (breakingScore > 0.7) return 'BREAKING';\n327\t  if (currentStatus === 'BREAKING') {\n328\t    if (shouldRetainBreaking(breakingScore, lastStatusChangeMinutes, growthPercent15)) {\n329\t      return 'BREAKING';\n330\t    }\n331\t    return 'TRENDING';\n332\t  }\n333\t\n334\t  // Trending: needs growth to stay trending (ported from TopicPulse tier3)\n335\t  if (currentStatus === 'TRENDING') {\n336\t    // TopicPulse: decay if 90-min growth < 8%. We use 60-min growth < 10%.\n337\t    if (growthPercent60 < 10 && lastStatusChangeMinutes > 60) {\n338\t      return 'ACTIVE'; // Explicit decay: trending → active\n339\t    }\n340\t    if (trendingScore > 0.4) return 'TRENDING';\n341\t    return 'ACTIVE';\n342\t  }\n343\t\n344\t  // New trending detection\n345\t  if (trendingScore > 0.5) return 'TRENDING';\n346\t  if (growthPercent15 > 50 && trendingScore > 0.3) return 'TRENDING';\n347\t\n348\t  // Age-based decay (ported from TopicPulse flat→stop→dead)\n349\t  if (ageMinutes > 48 * 60) return 'STALE';\n350\t  if (ageMinutes > 12 * 60) return 'ACTIVE';\n351\t  if (ageMinutes > 3 * 60) {\n352\t    // After 3 hours at ACTIVE with no growth → STALE\n353\t    if (currentStatus === 'ACTIVE' && lastStatusChangeMinutes > 180 && growthPercent60 < 5) {\n354\t      return 'STALE';\n355\t    }\n356\t    return 'ACTIVE';\n357\t  }\n358\t\n359\t  return currentStatus === 'EMERGING' ? 'EMERGING' : 'ACTIVE';\n360\t}\n361\t\n362\t// ─── Main Processing ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n363\t\n364\tasync function processScoring(job: Job<ScoringJob>): Promise<void> {\n365\t  const { storyId } = job.data;\n366\t\n367\t  logger.info({ storyId }, 'Scoring story');\n368\t\n369\t  const story = await prisma.story.findUnique({\n370\t    where: { id: storyId },\n371\t  });\n372\t\n373\t  if (!story) {\n374\t    logger.warn({ storyId }, 'Story not found, skipping scoring');\n375\t    return;\n376\t  }\n377\t\n378\t  // Calculate all scores\n379\t  const [breakingScore, trendingResult, confidenceScore, localityScore] = await Promise.all([\n380\t    calculateBreakingScore(storyId),\n381\t    calculateTrendingScore(storyId),\n382\t    calculateConfidenceScore(storyId),\n383\t    calculateLocalityScore(storyId),\n384\t  ]);\n385\t\n386\t  const trendingScore = trendingResult.score;\n387\t\n388\t  // Composite score\n389\t  const compositeScore =\n390\t    0.35 * breakingScore +\n391\t    0.25 * trendingScore +\n392\t    0.20 * confidenceScore +\n393\t    0.20 * localityScore;\n394\t\n395\t  // Determine status with tiered logic\n396\t  const ageMs = Date.now() - story.firstSeenAt.getTime();\n397\t  const ageMinutes = ageMs / (1000 * 60);\n398\t  const previousStatus = story.status;\n399\t\n400\t  // Time since last status change (for retention/decay logic)\n401\t  const lastStatusChangeMs = story.lastUpdatedAt\n402\t    ? Date.now() - story.lastUpdatedAt.getTime()\n403\t    : ageMs;\n404\t  const lastStatusChangeMinutes = lastStatusChangeMs / (1000 * 60);\n405\t\n406\t  const newStatus = determineStatus(\n407\t articleExtractionQueue: Queue;\n13\tlet geocodingQueue: Queue;\n14\tlet embeddingsQueue: Queue;\n15\tlet summarizationQueue: Queue;\n16\tlet sentimentQueue: Queue;\n17\tlet credibilityQueue: getSharedConnection();\n25\t\n26\t  if (!ingestionQueue) {\n27\t    ingestionQueue = new Queue('ingestion', { connection });\n28\t  }\n29\t  if (!scoringQueue) {\n30\t    scoringQueue = new Queue('scoring', { connection });\n31\t  }\n32\t  if (!llmIngestionQueue) {\n33\t    llmIngestionQueue = new Queue('llm-ingestion', { connection });\n34\t  }\n35\t  if (!articleExtractionQueue) {\n36\t    articleExtractionQueue = new Queue('article-extraction', { connection });\n37\t  }\n38\t  if (!geocodingQueue) {\n39\t    geocodingQueue = new Queue('geocoding', { connection });\n40\t  }\n41\t  if (!embeddingsQueue) {\n42\t    embeddingsQueue = new Queue('embeddings', { connection });\n43\t  }\n44\t  if (!summarizationQueue) {\n45\t    summarizationQueue = new Queue('summarization', { connection });\n46\t  }\n47\t  if (!sentimentQueue) {\n48\t    sentimentQueue = new Queue('sentiment', { connection });\n49\t  }\n50\t  if (!credibilityQueue) {\n51\t    credibilityQueue = new Queue('credibility', { connection });\n52\t  }\n53\t  if (!digestQueue) {\n54\t    digestQueue = new Queue('digest', { connection });\n55\t  }\n56\t\n57\t  return {\n58\t    ingestionQueue,\n59\t    scoringQueue,\n60\t    llmIngestionQueue,\n61\t    articleExtractionQueue,\n62\t    geocodingQueue,\n63\t    embeddingsQueue,\n64\t    summarizationQueue,\n65\t    sentimentQueue,\n66\t    credibilityQueue,\n67\t    digestQueue,\n68\t  };\n69\t}\n70\t\n71\t/**\n72\t * Schedule RSS feed polling jobs for all active RSS sources\n73\t */\n74\tasync function scheduleRSSPolls(): Promise<void> {\n75\t  const { ingestionQueue } = getQueues();\n76\t\n77\t  try {\n78\t    const rssSources = await prisma.source.findMany({\n79\t      where: {\n80\t        platform: 'RSS',\n81\t        isActive: true,\n82\t      },\n83\t    });\n84\t\n85\t    logger.info({ count: rssSources.length }, 'Scheduling RSS poll jobs');\n86\t\n87\t    for (const source of rssSources) {\n88\t      if (!source.url) {\n89\t        logger.warn({ sourceId: source.id, name: source.name }, 'RSS source has no URL, skipping');\n90\t        continue;\n91\t      }\n92\t\n93\t      await ingestionQueue.add(\n94\t        'rss_poll',\n95\t        {\n96\t          type: 'rss_poll',\n97\t          sourceId: source.id,\n98\t          feedUrl: source.url,\n99\t        },\n100\t        {\n101\t          jobId: `rss-poll-${source.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n102\t          attempts: 3,\n103\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n104\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 }, // Keep completed jobs for 1 hour\n105\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },    // Keep failed jobs for 24 hours\n106\t        }\n107\t      );\n108\t    }\n109\t  } catch (err) {\n110\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule RSS polls');\n111\t  }\n112\t}\n113\t\n114\t/**\n115\t * Schedule NewsAPI polling jobs for all active NewsAPI sources\n116\t */\n117\tasync function scheduleNewsAPIPolls(): Promise<void> {\n118\t  const { ingestionQueue } = getQueues();\n119\t\n120\t  try {\n121\t    const newsapiSources = await prisma.source.findMany({\n122\t      where: {\n123\t        platform: 'NEWSAPI',\n124\t        isActive: true,\n125\t      },\n126\t    });\n127\t\n128\t    logger.info({ count: newsapiSources.length }, 'Scheduling NewsAPI poll jobs');\n129\t\n130\t    for (const source of newsapiSources) {\n131\t      const metadata = source.metadata as Record<string, unknown> | null;\n132\t\n133\t      await ingestionQueue.add(\n134\t        'newsapi_poll',\n135\t        {\n136\t          type: 'newsapi_poll',\n137\t          sourceId: source.id,\n138\t          query: (metadata?.['query'] as string) || 'Houston Texas',\n139\t        },\n140\t        {\n141\t          jobId: `newsapi-poll-${source.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n142\t          attempts: 3,\n143\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n144\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n145\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n146\t        }\n147\t      );\n148\t    }\n149\t  } catch (err) {\n150\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule NewsAPI polls');\n151\t  }\n152\t}\n153\t\n154\t/**\n155\t * Schedule Facebook Page polling jobs for all active Facebook sources\n156\t */\n157\tasync function scheduleFacebookPagePolls(): Promise<void> {\n158\t  const { true,\n165\t      },\n166\t    });\n167\t\n168\t    logger.info({ count: fbSources.length }, 'Scheduling Facebook page poll jobs');\n169\t\n170\t    for (const source of fbSources) {\n171\t      if (!source.platformId) {\n172\t        logger.warn({ sourceId: source.id, name: source.name }, 'Facebook source has no platformId, skipping');\n173\t        continue;\n174\t      }\n175\t\n176\t      const metadata = source.metadata as Record<string, unknown> | null;\n177\t      const accessToken = (metadata?.['accessToken'] as string) || process.env['FACEBOOK_ACCESS_TOKEN'];\n178\t\n179\t      if (!accessToken) {\n180\t        logger.warn({ sourceId: source.id }, 'No access token available for Facebook source');\n181\t        continue;\n182\t      }\n183\t\n184\t      await type: 'exponential', delay: 10000 },\n196\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n197\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n198\t        }\n199\t      );\n200\t    }\n201\t  } catch (err) {\n202\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule Facebook page polls');\n203\t  }\n204\t}\n205\t\n206\t/**\n207\t * Schedule LLM polling jobs for all active LLM sources\n208\t */\n209\tasync function scheduleLLMPolls(): Promise<void> {\n210\t  const { llmIngestionQueue } = getQueues();\n211\t\n212\t  try {\n213\t    const llmSources = await prisma.source.findMany({\n214\t      where: {\n215\t        platform: { in: ['LLM_OPENAI', 'LLM_CLAUDE', 'LLM_GROK', 'LLM_GEMINI'] },\n216\t        isActive: true,\n217\t      },\n218\t      include: {\n219\t        market: true,\n220\t      },\n221\t    });\n222\t\n223\t    logger.info({ count: llmSources.length }, 'Scheduling LLM poll jobs');\n224\t\n225\t    for (const source of llmSources) {\n226\t      // Find the matching AccountCredential for this platform\n227\t      const credential = await prisma.accountCredential.findFirst({\n228\t        where: {\n229\t          platform: source.platform,\n230\t          isActive: true,\n231\t        },\n232\t      });\n233\t\n234\t      if (!credential?.apiKey) {\n235\t        logger.warn({ sourceId: source.id, platform: source.platform }, 'No API key found for LLM source, skipping');\n236\t        continue;\n237\t      }\n238\t\n239\t      const marketKeywords = source.market?.keywords as string[] | null;\n240\t\n241\t      await llmIngestionQueue.add(\n242\t        'llm_poll',\n243\t        {\n244\t          type: 'llm_poll',\n245\t          sourceId: source.id,\n246\t          platform: source.platform,\n247\t          marketName: source.market?.name || null,\n248\t          marketKeywords: marketKeywords || [],\n249\t          apiKey: credential.apiKey,\n250\t        },\n251\t        {\n252\t          jobId: `llm-poll-${source.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n253\t          attempts: 3,\n254\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 10000 },\n255\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n256\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n257\t        }\n258\t      );\n259\t    }\n260\t  } catch (err) {\n261\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule LLM polls');\n262\t  }\n263\t}\n264\t\n265\t/**\n266\t * Schedule article extraction jobs for posts with URLs but no extracted text\n267\t */\n268\tasync function scheduleArticleExtractions(): Promise<void> {\n269\t  const { articleExtractionQueue } = getQueues();\n270\t\n271\t  try {\n272\t    const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000);\n273\t\n274\t    const posts = await select: { id: true, url: true },\n281\t    });\n282\t\n283\t    logger.info({ count: posts.length }, 'Scheduling article extraction jobs');\n284\t\n285\t    for (const post of posts) {\n286\t        },\n293\t        {\n294\t          jobId: `article-extract-${post.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n295\t          attempts: 3,\n296\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n297\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n298\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n299\t        }\n300\t      );\n301\t    }\n302\t  } catch (err) {\n303\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule        backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n341\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n342\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n343\t        }\n344\t      );\n345\t    }\n346\t  } catch (err) {\n347\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule geocoding jobs');\n348\t  }\n349\t}\n350\t\n351\t/**\n352\t * Schedule embedding generation jobs for recent posts and stories\n353\t */\n354\tasync function scheduleEmbeddingJobs(): Promise<void> {\n355\t  const { embeddingsQueue } = getQueues();\n356\t\n357\t  try {\n358\t    const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000);\n359\t\n360\t    // Find source posts from the last hour with non-empty content\n361\t    const posts = await prisma.sourcePost.findMany({\n362\t      where: {\n363\t        createdAt: { gte: jobs');\n370\t\n371\t    for (const post of posts) {\n372\t      await embeddingsQueue.add(\n373\t        'embed_post',\n374\t        {\n375\t          type: 'embed_post',\n376\t          sourcePostId: post.id,\n377\t        },\n378\t        {\n379\t          jobId: `embed-post-${post.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n380\t          attempts: 3,\n381\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', last hour\n389\t    const stories = await prisma.story.findMany({\n390\t      where: {\n391\t        updatedAt: { gte: oneHourAgo },\n392\t      },\n393\t      select: { id: true },\n394\t    });\n395\t\n396\t    logger.info({ count: stories.length }, 'Scheduling story embedding jobs');\n397\t\n398\t    for (const story of stories) {\n399\t      await embeddingsQueue.add(\n400\t removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n411\t        }\n412\t      );\n413\t    }\n414\t  } catch (err) {\n415\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule embedding jobs');\n416\t  }\n417\t}\n418\t\n419\t/**\n420\t * Schedule summarization jobs for stories with enough sources but no summary\n421\t */\n422\tasync function scheduleSummarizationJobs(): Promise<void> {\n423\t  const  where: {\n430\t        sourceCount: { gte: 3 },\n431\t        OR: [\n432\t          { aiSummary: null },\n433\t          { aiSummaryAt: { lt: oneHourAgo } },\n434\t        ],\n435\t      },\n436\t      select: { id: true, sourceCount: true },\n437\t    });\n438\t\n439\t    logger.info({ count: stories.length }, 'Scheduling summarization jobs');\n440\t\n441\t    for (const story of stories) {\n449\t          jobId: `summarize-${story.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n450\t          attempts: 3,\n451\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 10000 },\n452\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n453\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n454\t        }\n455\t      );\n456\t    }\n457\t  } catch (err) {\n458\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule summarization jobs');\n459\t  }\n460\t}\n461\t\n462\t/**\n463\t * Schedule sentiment analysis jobs for recent posts without sentiment scores\n464\t */\n465\tasync function scheduleSentimentJobs(): Promise<void> {\n466\t  const { sentimentQueue } = getQueues();\n467\t\n468\t  try {\n469\t    const oneHourAgo = new Date(Date.now() - 60 * 60 * 1000);\n470\t\n471\t    const posts = await prisma.sourcePost.findMany({\n472\t      where: {\n473\t        createdAt: { gte: oneHourAgo },\n474\t        sentimentScore: null,\n475\t      },\n476\t      select: { id: true },\n477\t    });\n478\t\n479\t    logger.info({ count: posts.length }, 'Scheduling sentiment analysis jobs');\n480\t\n481\t    for (const post of posts) {\n482\t      await sentimentQueue.add(\n483\t        'analyze_sentiment',\n484\t        {\n485\t          type: 'analyze_sentiment',\n486\t          sourcePostId: post.id,\n487\t        },\n488\t        {\n489\t          jobId: `sentiment-${post.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n490\t          attempts: 3,\n491\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n492\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n493\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n494\t        }\n495\t      );\n496\t    }\n497\t  } catch (err) {\n498\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule sentiment jobs');\n499\t  }\n500\t}\n501\t\n502\t/**\n503\t * Schedule credibility score updates for all active sources (daily)\n504\t */\n505\tasync function scheduleCredibilityUpdates(): Promise<void> {\n506\t  const { credibilityQueue } = getQueues();\n507\t\n508\t  try {\n509\t    const sources = await prisma.source.findMany({\n510\t      where: {\n511\t        isActive: true,\n512\t      },\n513\t      select: { id: true, name: true },\n514\t    });\n515\t\n516\t    logger.info({ count: sources.length }, 'Scheduling credibility update jobs');\n517\t\n518\t    for (const source of sources) {\n519\t      await credibilityQueue.add(\n520\t        'update_credibility',\n521\t        {\n522\t          type: 'update_credibility',\n523\t          sourceId: source.id,\n524\t        },\n525\t        {\n526\t          jobId: `credibility-${source.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n527\t          attempts: 2,\n528\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 5000 },\n529\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 86400 },\n530\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n531\t        }\n532\t      );\n533\t    }\n534\t  } catch (err) {\n535\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule credibility updates');\n536\t  }\n537\t}\n538\t\n539\t/**\n540\t * Schedule digest email jobs for subscriptions that are due\n541\t */\n542\tasync function scheduleDigests(): Promise<void> {\n543\t  const { digestQueue } = getQueues();\n544\t\n545\t  try {\n546\t    const now = new Date();\n547\t\n548\t    const subscriptions = await prisma.digestSubscription.findMany({\n549\t      where: {\n550\t        isActive: true,\n551\t      },\n552\t    });\n553\t\n554\t    // Filter to only subscriptions that are due based on frequency and lastSentAt\n555\t    const dueSubscriptions = subscriptions.filter((sub) => {\n556\t      if (!sub.lastSentAt) return true; // Never sent, so it's due\n557\t\n558\t      const lastSent = sub.lastSentAt.getTime();\n559\t      const elapsed = now.getTime() - lastSent;\n560\t\n561\t      switch (sub.frequency) {\n562\t        case 'HOURLY':\n563\t          return elapsed >= 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 hour\n564\t        case 'TWICE_DAILY':\n565\t          return elapsed >= 12 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 12 hours\n566\t        case 'DAILY':\n567\t          return elapsed >= 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 24 hours\n568\t        case 'WEEKLY':\n569\t          return elapsed >= 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 7 days\n570\t        default:\n571\t          return false;\n572\t      }\n573\t    });\n574\t\n575\t    logger.info({ count: dueSubscriptions.length, total: subscriptions.length }, 'Scheduling digest jobs');\n576\t\n577\t    for (const sub of dueSubscriptions) {\n578\t      await digestQueue.add(\n579\t        'send_digest',\n580\t        {\n581\t          type: 'send_digest',\n582\t          subscriptionId: sub.id,\n583\t          accountId: sub.accountId,\n584\t          userId: sub.userId,\n585\t          email: sub.email,\n586\t          frequency: sub.frequency,\n587\t          timezone: sub.timezone,\n588\t          filters: sub.filters,\n589\t        },\n590\t        {\n591\t          jobId: `digest-${sub.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n592\t          attempts: 3,\n593\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 10000 },\n594\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 3600 },\n595\t          removeOnFail: { age: 86400 },\n596\t        }\n597\t      );\n598\t    }\n599\t  } catch (err) {\n600\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to schedule digests');\n601\t  }\n602\t}\n603\t\n604\t/**\n605\t * Re-score all non-archived stories to apply score decay\n606\t */\n607\tasync function runScoreDecay(): Promise<void> {\n608\t  const { scoringQueue } = getQueues();\n609\t\n610\t  try {\n611\t    const activeStories = await prisma.story.findMany({\n612\t      where: {\n613\t        status: { notIn: ['ARCHIVED', 'STALE'] },\n614\t      },\n615\t      select: { id: true },\n616\t    });\n617\t\n618\t    logger.info({ count: activeStories.length }, 'Scheduling score decay re-scoring');\n619\t\n620\t    for (const story of activeStories) {\n621\t      await scoringQueue.add(\n622\t        'score',\n623\t        { storyId: story.id },\n624\t        {\n625\t          jobId: `decay-score-${story.id}-${Date.now()}`,\n626\t          attempts: 2,\n627\t          backoff: { type: 'exponential', delay: 2000 },\n628\t          removeOnComplete: { age: 1800 },\n629\t          removeOnFail: { age: 3600 },\n630\t        }\n631\t      );\n632\t    }\n633\t  } catch (err) {\n634\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to run score decay');\n635\t  }\n636\t}\n637\t\n638\t/**\n639\t * Archive stories older than 72 hours with no recent activity\n640\t */\n641\tasync function runCleanup(): Promise<void> {\n642\t  try {\n643\t    const cutoff = new Date(Date.now() - 72 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 72 hours ago\n644\t\n645\t    const result = await prisma.story.updateMany({\n646\t      where: {\n647\t        status: { notIn: ['ARCHIVED'] },\n648\t        lastUpdatedAt: { lt: cutoff },\n649\t      },\n650\t      data: {\n651\t        status: 'ARCHIVED',\n652\t      },\n653\t    });\n654\t\n655\t    logger.info({ archivedCount: result.count }, 'Cleanup complete: archived old stories');\n656\t  } catch (err) {\n657\t    logger.error({ err }, 'Failed to run cleanup');\n658\t  }\n659\t}\n660\t\n661\t// Interval handles for cleanup on shutdown\n662\tconst intervals: NodeJS.Timeout[] = [];\n663\t\n664\t/**\n665\t * Set up all recurring scheduled jobs\n666\t */\n667\texport function startSchedulers(): void {\n668\t  logger.info('Starting poll schedulers');\n669\t\n670\t  // RSS feeds: every 2 minutes\n671\t  const rssInterval = setInterval(scheduleRSSPolls, 2 * 60 * 1000);\n672\t  intervals.push(rssInterval);\n673\t\n674\t  // NewsAPI: every 3 minutes\n675\t  const newsapiInterval = setInterval(scheduleNewsAPIPolls, 3 * 60 * 1000);\n676\t  intervals.push(newsapiInterval);\n677\t\n678\t  // Facebook Pages: every 5 minutes\n679\t  const fbInterval = setInterval(scheduleFacebookPagePolls, 5 * 60 * 1000);\n680\t  intervals.push(fbInterval);\n681\t\n682\t  // Score decay: every 10 minutes\n683\t  const decayInterval = setInterval(runScoreDecay, 10 * 60 * 1000);\n684\t  intervals.push(decayInterval);\n685\t\n686\t  // Cleanup: every hour\n687\t  const cleanupInterval = setInterval(runCleanup, 60 * 60 * 1000);\n688\t  intervals.push(cleanupInterval);\n689\t\n690\t  // LLM polls: every 10 minutes\n691\t  const llmInterval = setInterval(scheduleLLMPolls, 10 * 60 * 1000);\n692\t  intervals.push(llmInterval);\n693\t\n694\t  // Article extraction: every 5 minutes\n695\t  const articleExtractionInterval = setInterval(scheduleArticleExtractions, 5 * 60 * 1000);\n696\t  intervals.push(articleExtractionInterval);\n697\t\n698\t  // Geocoding: every 15 minutes\n699\t         },\n87\t          },\n88\t        };\n89\t      }\n90\t    }\n91\t\n92\t    if (minScore !== undefined) {\n93\t      where.compositeScore = { gte: minScore };\n94\t    }\n95\t\n96\t    if Let me produce the plan.\n\n---\n\n## Comprehensive Implementation Plan: TPHyperlocal News Desk Platform\n\n### Current State Assessment\n\n**What exists today:**\n- Multi-tenant account/market/user model (Prisma/PostgreSQL)\n- Ingestion workers for RSS, NewsAPI, Facebook Pages, and LLM providers (OpenAI, Claude, Grok, Gemini)\n- BullMQ-based pipeline: ingestion -> enrichment -> clustering -> scoring -> notification\n- 14 workers covering ingestion, enrichment, scoring, embeddings, sentiment, summarization, geocoding, article extraction, credibility, clustering, digest, notification, RSS discovery\n- Scheduler polling RSS (2m), NewsAPI (3m), Facebook (5m), LLMs (10m), with score decay and cleanup\n- Scoring worker with TopicPulse-inspired tiered status logic (EMERGING, BREAKING, TRENDING, ACTIVE, STALE, ARCHIVED) and category decay curves\n- Admin UI for sources with platform selector, trust scores, market assignment\n- Admin pages for credentials, markets\n- Stories API with faceted filtering, breaking/trending endpoints\n- Frontend dashboard, story detail, feeds, settings pages\n\n**What the current StoryStatus enum provides:** EMERGING, BREAKING, TRENDING, ACTIVE, STALE, ARCHIVED\n\n**What the new editorial state model requires:** ALERT, BREAKING, DEVELOPING, TOP_STORY, ONGOING, FOLLOW_UP, STALE, ARCHIVED\n\n**Key gap:** The current system conflates algorithmic scoring states with editorial states. The new model separates these concerns -- the scoring engine produces numeric scores, and the editorial state model is a distinct lifecycle that editors can control.\n\n---\n\n## Phase 1: Editorial State Model and Scoring Refactor\n\n**Goal:** Replace the current StoryStatus enum with the new editorial state model while preserving backward compatibility. Make the scoring engine feed into the editorial state machine rather than directly setting status.\n\n**What gets built:**\n- New `EditorialState` enum: ALERT, BREAKING, DEVELOPING, TOP_STORY, ONGOING, FOLLOW_UP, STALE, ARCHIVED\n- A `StoryStateTransition` model to track all state changes (who/what triggered them, timestamp)\n- Refactored scoring worker that recommends state transitions rather than directly writing status\n- State machine logic enforcing valid transitions (e.g., ALERT can only go to BREAKING or DEVELOPING; STALE cannot jump to ALERT without re-scoring)\n- Auto-promotion rules: the system can auto-transition stories based on score thresholds, but editors can override\n- A `stateOverride` field on Story so editorial decisions take precedence over algorithmic ones\n- API endpoints for manual state transitions (editor actions)\n\n**Schema changes:**\n```\n// Replace StoryStatus enum\nenum EditorialState {\n  ALERT       // Just detected, needs immediate editorial attention\n  BREAKING    // Confirmed breaking, actively covering  \n  DEVELOPING  // Story is developing, new info coming in\n  TOP_STORY   // Editor-promoted to top story\n  ONGOING     // Long-running story, not breaking but active\n  FOLLOW_UP   // Related to a prior story\n  STALE       // No new activity, aging out\n  ARCHIVED    // Completed lifecycle\n}\n\n// New model\nmodel StoryStateTransition {\n  id            String         @id @default(cuid())\n  storyId       String\n  story         Story          @relation(...)\n  fromState     EditorialState\n  toState       EditorialState\n  trigger       String         // \"AUTO_SCORE\", \"EDITOR\", \"TIMER\", \"MERGE\"\n  triggeredBy   String?        // userId if editor\n  reason        String?        // \"breakingScore exceeded 0.7\", \"editor promoted\"\n  metadata      Json?\n  createdAt     DateTime       @default(now())\n  @@index([storyId, createdAt(sort: Desc)])\n}\n\n// Story model additions\nmodel Story {\n  // ... existing fields ...\n  editorialState    EditorialState  @default(ALERT)\n  stateOverride     Boolean         @default(false)  // true if editor manually set state\n  lastStateChangeAt DateTime        @default(now())\n  stateTransitions  StoryStateTransition[]\n}\n```\n\n**Files to create/modify:**\n- `breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma` -- new enum, StoryStateTransition model, Story field changes\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/lib/state-machine.ts` -- new file: editorial state machine with valid transitions, auto-transition rules\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/workers/scoring.worker.ts` -- refactor `determineStatus()` to produce state recommendations via the state machine\n- `breaking-news/backend/src/routes/stories.ts` -- update queries for new enum, add PATCH endpoint for editorial state transitions\n- `breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/editor.ts` -- new/updated routes for state management\n- `breaking-news/frontend/src/app/page.tsx` -- update dashboard to show new states\n- `breaking-news/frontend/src/app/stories/[id]/page.tsx` -- add state transition controls\n\n**Estimated complexity:** L (Large) -- touches the core data model and scoring pipeline, requires migration of existing data from old enum to new enum.\n\n---\n\n## Phase 2: Twitter/X API v2 Integration\n\n**Goal:** Add Twitter/X as a first-class real-time source with proper API v2 support, including filtered stream and search endpoints.\n\n**What gets built:**\n- Twitter/X ingestion handler in the ingestion worker (alongside existing RSS, NewsAPI, Facebook handlers)\n- Support for two modes: (a) filtered stream for real-time breaking news keywords, (b) recent search for periodic polling\n- Twitter-specific fields on SourcePost: tweet ID, retweet count, quote count, reply count, bookmark count\n- Rate limit management with exponential backoff (Twitter v2 has strict rate limits)\n- Credential management: OAuth 2.0 Bearer Token stored in AccountCredential\n- Admin UI additions for Twitter source configuration: search query, stream rules, list ID\n\n**Schema changes:**\n- Add `TWITTER_STREAM` to Platform enum (distinguish stream vs poll)\n- SourcePost already has engagement fields; add `engagementBookmarks Int @default(0)` and `engagementQuotes Int @default(0)` for Twitter-specific metrics\n\n**Files to create/modify:**\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/workers/ingestion.worker.ts` -- add `handleTwitterSearchPoll()` handler\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/workers/twitter-stream.worker.ts` -- new file: persistent filtered stream connection using Twitter v2 streaming API\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/lib/twitter-client.ts` -- new file: Twitter API v2 client with auth, rate limiting, retry logic\n- `breaking-news/worker/src/schedulers/poll-scheduler.ts` -- add `scheduleTwitterPolls()` interval\n- same pattern, plus the stream worker is new infrastructure.\n\n---\n\n## Phase 3: Grok (xAI) Real-Time Breaking News\n\n**Goal:** Use Grok's unique real-time knowledge (from X/Twitter data) as a dedicated breaking news source, distinct from the general LLM polling.\n\n**What gets built:**\n- Dedicated Grok breaking news worker that queries xAI's API specifically for emerging local news models, a new worker, LLM factory abstraction, and significant UI additions.\n\n---\n\n## Phase 6: Admin Source Configuration Overhaul\n\n**Goal:** Make all source types (including Twitter, Facebook, poll interval override (already modeled in `AccountSource.pollIntervalMs` but not wired up)\n- Source health dashboard: success/failure rates, average latency, last error, posts per hour\n- Credential binding UI: link specific AccountCredentials to specific sources\n- Source testing: \"Test Connection\" button that runs a one-off poll and shows results\n- Bulk operations: enable/disable multiple sources, bulk trust score adjustment\n- Source templates: pre-built source configurations for common setups (\"Houston TV Stations RSS Bundle\")\n\n**Schema changes:**\n```\nmodel SourceHealthLog {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  sourceId    String\n  success     Boolean\n  latencyMs   Int\n  postCount   Int      @default(0)\n  error       String?\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  @@index([sourceId, createdAt(sort: Desc)])\n}\n\nmodel SourceTemplate {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  name        String\n  description String?\n  platform    Platform\n  sources     Json     // array of { name, url, sourceType, trustScore }\n  isPublic    Boolean  @default(false)\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n}\n```\n\n**Files to @default(cuid())\n  domain       String  @unique\n  score        Float   @default(0)\n  appearances  Int     @default(0)\n  viralAppearances Int @default(0)\n  updatedAt    DateTime @updatedAt\n  @@index([domain])\n}\n\nmodel ScoringAlgorithm {\n  id          String  @id @default(cuid())\n  accountId   String?\n  name        String\n  parameters  Json    // { tier1_hot_score, tier1_trending_score, tier2_retrospective_minutes, ... }\n  isDefault   Boolean @default(false)\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n```\n\n**Files to ─────── independent source  \n   ├── Phase 4 (Facebook) ──── extends existing source\n   |\n   ├── Phase 5 (First Draft) ── depends on Phase 1 states\n   |      |\n   |      └── Phase 9 (Bookmarks/UX) ── can partially parallel\n   |\n   ├── Phase 6 (Admin Config) ── enhances Phases 2-4\n   |\n   ├── Phase 7 (Scoring Parity) ── refines Phase 1\n   |      |\n   |      └── Phase 8 (Distribution) ── needs scoring + states\n   |\n   └── Phase 10 (Search/Analytics) ── benefits from all prior phases\n```\n\nPhases 2, 3, and 4 (social sources) can be built in parallel after Phase 1. Phase 5 (First Draft) can begin as soon as Phase 1 is complete. Phase 6 can be woven in anytime. Phases 7-10 build on the earlier foundations.\n\n---\n\n## Features NOT Included (Deferred or Unnecessary)\n\nThe following TopicPulse features are intentionally excluded from this plan as they are either low-impact, vendor-specific, or premature:\n\n- **NetSuite Integration (#36)** -- ERP integration, not relevant to news desk\n- **FreshDesk Integration (#37)** -- support tooling, not core product\n- **InstantVideo/Wibbitz (#19, #20)** -- video rebranding is a separate product vertical\n- **SSO/SAML (#53)** -- enterprise feature, add when needed\n- **Stocks Integration (#26)** -- niche, add in a future financial news vertical\n- **RadioGPT (#13)** -- broadcast-specific, not general news desk\n- **ShowPrep (#25), PrepOS (#40), History of the Day (#41)** -- broadcast content prep, defer\n- **MongoDB (#57)** -- the PostgreSQL + OpenSearch stack covers all needs\n- **Dual Database Architecture (#58)** -- premature optimization;
