Let me build the implementation plan.\n\n---\n\n# TPHyperlocal News Desk Platform -- Phased Implementation Plan\n\n## Current State Assessment\n\n**What exists today:**\n- Multi-tenant architecture with Account, Market, User, Source models (Prisma/PostgreSQL)\n- BullMQ worker pipeline: ingestion (RSS, NewsAPI, Facebook), enrichment, scoring, clustering, embeddings, sentiment, summarization, geocoding, article extraction, credibility, digests, notifications\n- Scoring engine with TopicPulse-inspired tiered decay logic (breaking/trending/confidence/locality/composite)\n- 6-state story lifecycle: EMERGING, BREAKING, TRENDING, ACTIVE, STALE, ARCHIVED\n- Admin UI for sources, markets, credentials\n- Editor workflow (PATCH edit, revert, review status)\n- Stories API with faceted filtering, breaking/trending endpoints\n- LLM ingestion worker supporting OpenAI, Claude, Grok, Gemini\n- RSS feed generation, webhook subscriptions, digest subscriptions\n\n**What is missing (from the 69-feature inventory):**\n- 46 features with no equivalent, 22 partial\n- No Twitter/X API v2 ingestion worker (enum exists, no handler)\n- No Grok (xAI) real-time breaking detection\n- No editorial state model with ALERT/DEVELOPING/TOP_STORY/ONGOING/FOLLOW_UP states\n- No FirstDraft AI content generation (summaries, rewrites, tweets, bullets, idea starters)\n- No LLM Factory abstraction\n- No UniversalPromptManager\n- No MyVoice custom writing styles\n- No CommunityRadar social monitoring\n- No Smart Pulses / Vector Pulses\n- No ShowPrep / PrepOS\n- No web widgets or embeddable feeds\n- No push notifications (Firebase)\n- No feature flags system\n- No Redis caching layer\n- No Elasticsearch/OpenSearch integration\n- No bookmarks, content streams, or Glance summaries\n\n---\n\n## Phase 1: Editorial State Model + Social Source Ingestion\n**Goal:** Expand the story lifecycle to match a professional news desk and bring in Twitter/X + Grok as real-time sources.\n**Estimated Complexity:** L\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**1a. Extended Editorial State Model**\n- Replace the current 6-state `StoryStatus` enum with the 8-state model: `ALERT`, `BREAKING`, `DEVELOPING`, `TOP_STORY`, `ONGOING`, `FOLLOW_UP`, `STALE`, `ARCHIVED`\n- Add `editorialState` field to Story (separate from the auto-computed `status`) plus `editorialStateSetBy`, `editorialStateSetAt` to allow editors to override\n- Add `stateTransitionLog` as a new model to track every state change with timestamp, actor (system vs editor), and reason\n- Update the scoring worker `determineStatus()` to map its computed output to the new states: current EMERGING maps to DEVELOPING, current BREAKING stays BREAKING but can be promoted to ALERT by editors, TRENDING maps to TOP_STORY, ACTIVE maps to ONGOING, and add time-based transitions to FOLLOW_UP\n- Add migration for STALE stories older than configurable threshold to ARCHIVED\n\n**1b. Twitter/X API v2 Ingestion**\n- New ingestion handler `handleTwitterPoll` in `ingestion.worker.ts` (alongside existing RSS, NewsAPI, Facebook handlers)\n- Support Twitter API v2 filtered stream (real-time) and search/recent (polling) endpoints\n- Use `AccountCredential` with platform `TWITTER` for Bearer tokens\n- Map Twitter engagement (likes, retweets, replies, quote tweets) to `SourcePost` engagement fields\n- Respect rate limits (450 requests/15min for search, streaming has its own limits)\n- Parse Twitter entities (hashtags, mentions, URLs) into `SourcePost.entities` JSON field\n\n**1c. Grok (xAI) Real-Time Breaking Detection**\n- Enhance the existing `llm-ingestion.worker.ts` Grok path with a specialized \"breaking news monitor\" prompt\n- Add a faster poll interval for Grok (every 2 minutes vs 10 minutes for other LLMs) since xAI Grok has real-time X/Twitter data access\n- Add a `breakingDetection` flag on LLM sources to distinguish \"analysis\" LLM sources from \"detection\" sources\n- When Grok detects a breaking event, auto-set story editorial state to ALERT with confidence threshold\n\n**1d. Admin UI for Social Sources**\n- Extend the existing sources admin page to support Twitter-specific configuration (search queries, tracked accounts, lists, stream rules)\n- Add Grok-specific configuration (breaking detection enabled, poll frequency override)\n- Add credential management flows for Twitter OAuth 2.0 Bearer tokens\n\n### Schema Changes\n\n```\n// Enum change\nenum StoryStatus {\n  ALERT        // Editor-confirmed, highest urgency (was not present)\n  BREAKING     // Auto-detected or editor-set breaking news\n  DEVELOPING   // Story still gathering sources (replaces EMERGING)\n  TOP_STORY    // High engagement/trending (replaces TRENDING)\n  ONGOING      // Active story past peak (replaces ACTIVE)\n  FOLLOW_UP    // Related to previous breaking/top story (new)\n  STALE        // No new activity\n  ARCHIVED     // Expired\n}\n\n// New model\nmodel StoryStateTransition {\n  id              String   @id @default(cuid())\n  storyId         String\n  story           Story    @relation(...)\n  fromState       StoryStatus\n  toState         StoryStatus\n  trigger         String   // \"SYSTEM_SCORING\", \"EDITOR_OVERRIDE\", \"TIME_DECAY\", \"GROK_ALERT\"\n  triggeredBy     String?  // userId if editor\n  reason          String?  // human-readable reason\n  metadata        Json?    // scoring data at time of transition\n  createdAt       DateTime @default(now())\n}\n\n// Story model additions\nmodel Story {\n  // ... existing fields ...\n  editorialOverride  Boolean  @default(false) // true = system scoring won't auto-change state\n  parentStoryId      String?  // for FOLLOW_UP stories linking to original\n  parentStory        Story?   @relation(\"StoryFollowUp\", ...)\n  followUps          Story[]  @relation(\"StoryFollowUp\")\n  stateTransitions   StoryStateTransition[]\n}\n\n// Source model additions for Twitter\n// (metadata Json field already exists, used for Twitter stream rules, search queries)\n```\n\n### Files to Create/Modify\n\n**Create:**\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/twitter-ingestion.worker.ts` -- Twitter API v2 handler\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/twitter-client.ts` -- Twitter API v2 client (auth, rate limiting, streaming)\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/editorial.ts` -- Editorial state override endpoints\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/sources/twitter-config.tsx` -- Twitter source configuration component\n\n**Modify:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma` -- New enum values, StoryStateTransition model, Story fields\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/scoring.worker.ts` -- Update `determineStatus()` for 8-state model\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/ingestion.worker.ts` -- Add Twitter dispatch case\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/llm-ingestion.worker.ts` -- Add Grok breaking detection mode\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/schedulers/poll-scheduler.ts` -- Add Twitter polling schedule, faster Grok schedule\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/stories.ts` -- Update status filters for new enum values\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/index.ts` -- Register editorial routes\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/sources/page.tsx` -- Add TWITTER_STREAM platform option, Grok breaking detection toggle\n\n---\n\n## Phase 2: LLM Factory + FirstDraft AI Content Generation\n**Goal:** Build the multi-LLM abstraction and AI-powered content generation that makes the news desk productive.\n**Estimated Complexity:** L\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**2a. LLM Factory (Multi-LLM Abstraction)**\n- Factory pattern supporting OpenAI (GPT-4o), Anthropic (Claude), xAI (Grok), Google (Gemini)\n- Unified interface: `generate(prompt, options) => { text, model, tokens, cost }`\n- Per-account credential resolution from `AccountCredential` table\n- Automatic fallback chain: if primary LLM fails, try secondary\n- Token counting, cost tracking, rate limit handling per provider\n- Streaming support for real-time generation\n\n**2b. UniversalPromptManager**\n- New `Prompt` and `PromptVersion` models for versioned prompt templates\n- Default prompts seeded for each content type (summary, short_summary, rewrite, tweet, bullets, idea_starter)\n- Per-account prompt customization (override defaults)\n- Variable interpolation: `{{story_title}}`, `{{story_content}}`, `{{market_name}}`, `{{voice_style}}`\n- Admin UI for editing prompts with preview\n\n**2c. FirstDraft Content Generation**\n- Port TopicPulse's FirstDraft types: summary, short_summary, rewrite, tweet, bullets, idea_starter\n- New `FirstDraft` model to cache generated content per story per type\n- Background worker that auto-generates summaries when stories reach BREAKING or TOP_STORY\n- API endpoints: `POST /api/v1/stories/:id/first-draft` (generate), `GET /api/v1/stories/:id/first-drafts` (list cached)\n- Frontend component showing generated content with copy-to-clipboard, regenerate button\n\n**2d. MyVoice Custom Writing Styles**\n- New `Voice` model: name, system prompt, sample text, interests, tone descriptors\n- Per-account voice library\n- FirstDraft generation can specify a voice, which modifies the system prompt\n- Admin UI for creating/editing voices\n\n### Schema Changes\n\n```\nmodel Prompt {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  accountId   String?  // null = system default\n  name        String   // \"summary\", \"tweet\", \"rewrite\", etc.\n  type        String   // \"first_draft\", \"idea_starter\", \"notification\"\n  template    String   @db.Text\n  variables   Json     // list of available variables\n  isDefault   Boolean  @default(false)\n  version     Int      @default(1)\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n\nmodel FirstDraft {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  storyId     String\n  story       Story    @relation(...)\n  userId      String?\n  type        String   // summary, short_summary, rewrite, tweet, bullets, idea_starter\n  voiceId     String?\n  content     String   @db.Text\n  model       String   // which LLM generated it\n  promptId    String?\n  tokens      Int?\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n\nmodel Voice {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  accountId   String\n  name        String\n  systemPrompt String  @db.Text\n  sampleText  String?  @db.Text\n  interests   Json?\n  tone        Json?    // [\"professional\", \"conversational\"]\n  isDefault   Boolean  @default(false)\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Create/Modify\n\n**Create:**\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/llm-factory.ts` -- LLM factory with provider adapters\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/llm-providers/openai.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/llm-providers/anthropic.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/llm-providers/xai.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/llm-providers/gemini.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/lib/prompt-manager.ts` -- Prompt resolution and interpolation\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/first-draft.worker.ts` -- Background generation worker\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/first-draft.ts` -- API endpoints\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/prompts.ts` -- Prompt management\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/voices.ts` -- Voice management\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/stories/[id]/first-draft-panel.tsx` -- UI component\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/prompts/page.tsx` -- Prompt editor\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/voices/page.tsx` -- Voice editor\n\n**Modify:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma` -- New models\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/llm-ingestion.worker.ts` -- Use LLM Factory instead of inline API calls\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/summarization.worker.ts` -- Use LLM Factory + PromptManager\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/schedulers/poll-scheduler.ts` -- Add first-draft scheduling\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/index.ts` -- Register new admin routes\n\n---\n\n## Phase 3: CommunityRadar Social Monitoring + Facebook Groups\n**Goal:** Deep social media monitoring for community sentiment and engagement, ported from TopicPulse.\n**Estimated Complexity:** M\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**3a. CommunityRadar Engine**\n- Social media monitoring system that tracks Facebook pages, Facebook groups, and Twitter accounts/lists for community mentions and sentiment\n- New `CommunityRadarConfig` model per account defining monitored URLs, scrape frequency, and content filters\n- `CommunityRadarPost` model for scraped social content with sentiment, engagement, and story correlation\n- Background worker that scrapes configured URLs on schedule using the existing ingestion patterns\n- Summarization worker that generates periodic community sentiment reports using the LLM Factory from Phase 2\n\n**3b. Facebook Groups Integration**\n- Extend `ingestion.worker.ts` with `facebook_group_poll` handler\n- Facebook Graph API v18.0 group posts endpoint with member count, engagement metrics\n- Group summary generation (daily/weekly) using LLM Factory\n- New `FacebookGroup` and `FacebookGroupSummary` models\n\n**3c. CommunityRadar API + Dashboard**\n- API endpoints: `GET /api/v1/community-radar/posts`, `GET /api/v1/community-radar/summary`, `GET /api/v1/community-radar/sentiment`\n- Dashboard page showing community pulse: top posts, trending topics, sentiment trend chart\n- Story correlation: link community posts to existing stories when content overlaps\n\n### Schema Changes\n\n```\nmodel CommunityRadarConfig {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  accountId   String\n  name        String\n  platform    Platform\n  url         String\n  urlType     String   // \"FB_PAGE\", \"FB_GROUP\", \"TWITTER_LIST\", \"TWITTER_SEARCH\"\n  scrapeFrequencyMin Int @default(120)\n  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)\n  lastScrapedAt DateTime?\n  metadata    Json?\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n\nmodel CommunityRadarPost {\n  id              String   @id @default(cuid())\n  configId        String\n  config          CommunityRadarConfig @relation(...)\n  platformPostId  String   @unique\n  content         String   @db.Text\n  authorName      String?\n  engagementScore Float    @default(0)\n  sentimentScore  Float?\n  sentimentLabel  String?\n  storyId         String?  // correlated story\n  story           Story?   @relation(...)\n  postedAt        DateTime\n  scrapedAt       DateTime @default(now())\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Create/Modify\n\n**Create:**\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/community-radar.worker.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/community-radar.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/community-radar.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/community/page.tsx` -- Community radar dashboard\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/community-radar/page.tsx` -- Config UI\n\n**Modify:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/schedulers/poll-scheduler.ts` -- Add community radar scheduling\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/ingestion.worker.ts` -- Add facebook_group_poll handler\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/index.ts`\n\n---\n\n## Phase 4: Redis Cache Layer + Feature Flags + Performance\n**Goal:** Production hardening for scale -- caching, feature flags, and search.\n**Estimated Complexity:** M\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**4a. Redis Cache Layer**\n- Centralized caching service wrapping the existing Redis connection (`/backend/src/lib/redis.ts`)\n- Cache strategies: TTL-based for stories list (30s), breaking stories (10s), facets (60s), community radar (120s)\n- Cache invalidation on story update, state transition, new source post ingestion\n- Cache-aside pattern in all hot API routes (stories list, breaking, trending, facets)\n\n**4b. Feature Flags System**\n- New `FeatureFlag` model with per-account and per-user granularity\n- Flags for: `firstDraft`, `communityRadar`, `grokBreaking`, `twitterIngestion`, `smartPulses`, `widgets`\n- Server-side flag evaluation in route middleware\n- Client-side flag provider via `/api/v1/features` endpoint\n- Admin UI for managing flags\n\n**4c. Elasticsearch/OpenSearch Integration (optional but high-impact)**\n- Index stories and source posts for full-text search\n- Replace the raw SQL source facet query in `stories.ts` with aggregation queries\n- Power the search route (`/backend/src/routes/search.ts`) with proper relevance ranking\n- Sync worker that indexes new/updated stories into OpenSearch\n\n### Schema Changes\n\n```\nmodel FeatureFlag {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  name        String   @unique\n  description String?\n  defaultValue Boolean @default(false)\n  overrides   Json?    // { accounts: { \"acc1\": true }, users: { \"user1\": false } }\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Create/Modify\n\n**Create:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/lib/cache.ts` -- Redis cache service\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/lib/feature-flags.ts` -- Flag evaluation\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/features.ts` -- Client-side flag endpoint\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/feature-flags.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/search-indexer.worker.ts` -- OpenSearch sync\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/lib/feature-flags.tsx` -- React context provider\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/admin/features/page.tsx`\n\n**Modify:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/stories.ts` -- Add caching\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/search.ts` -- Use OpenSearch\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/lib/redis.ts` -- Expose cache utilities\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/index.ts`\n\n---\n\n## Phase 5: Push Notifications + Content Distribution\n**Goal:** Get stories to users through push, Slack, email, and webhooks with TopicPulse-grade distribution.\n**Estimated Complexity:** M\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**5a. Firebase Cloud Messaging**\n- Device registration model and API endpoints\n- Push notification worker triggered by story state transitions (ALERT, BREAKING)\n- Per-user notification preferences (which categories, minimum score)\n- Web push and mobile push support\n\n**5b. Enhanced Slack Integration**\n- Extend existing notification model with Slack bot integration\n- Configurable Slack channels per category/state (e.g., #breaking-news gets ALERT+BREAKING, #daily-digest gets TOP_STORY)\n- Rich Slack message formatting with story card, sources, sentiment indicator\n- Slash command support for querying stories from Slack\n\n**5c. Enhanced Email Digests**\n- HTML email templates with story cards, images, sentiment badges\n- Per-user digest preferences with category/market filtering\n- \"Top stories\" automated email using the same logic as TopicPulse's `send_top_stories_to_email.php`\n\n**5d. Content Distribution Orchestrator**\n- Central service that routes story state transitions to the appropriate channels\n- Configurable rules: \"When story reaches ALERT, send push + Slack + email to configured recipients\"\n- Deduplication: don't re-notify for the same story within configurable cooldown\n\n### Schema Changes\n\n```\nmodel Device {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  userId      String\n  user        User     @relation(...)\n  token       String   @unique // FCM token\n  platform    String   // \"web\", \"ios\", \"android\"\n  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)\n  lastSeenAt  DateTime?\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n}\n\nmodel NotificationPreference {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  userId      String\n  accountId   String\n  channels    Json     // [\"push\", \"email\", \"slack\"]\n  categories  Json?    // null = all\n  minStates   Json     // [\"ALERT\", \"BREAKING\"]\n  minScore    Float    @default(0.5)\n  quietHours  Json?    // { start: \"22:00\", end: \"07:00\", timezone: \"America/Chicago\" }\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n\nmodel SlackIntegration {\n  id          String   @id @default(cuid())\n  accountId   String\n  channelId   String\n  channelName String\n  webhookUrl  String\n  states      Json     // which story states trigger this channel\n  categories  Json?\n  isActive    Boolean  @default(true)\n  createdAt   DateTime @default(now())\n  updatedAt   DateTime @updatedAt\n}\n```\n\n### Files to Create/Modify\n\n**Create:**\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/push-notification.worker.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/slack-notification.worker.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/distribution.worker.ts` -- Orchestrator\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/lib/firebase.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/devices.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/notification-preferences.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/slack.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/frontend/src/app/settings/notifications/page.tsx`\n\n**Modify:**\n- `/breaking-news/backend/prisma/schema.prisma`\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/notification.worker.ts` -- Refactor to use distribution orchestrator\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/workers/digest.worker.ts` -- Enhanced email templates\n- `/breaking-news/worker/src/schedulers/poll-scheduler.ts`\n- `/breaking-news/backend/src/routes/admin/index.ts`\n\n---\n\n## Phase 6: Smart Pulses, Bookmarks, ShowPrep + Broadcast Features\n**Goal:** Port TopicPulse's broadcast-specific features that make this a real newsroom tool.\n**Estimated Complexity:** L\n\n### What Gets Built\n\n**6a. Smart Pulses**\n- AI-powered topic feeds that dynamically select stories based on user interests, engagement patterns, and market relevance\n- Uses embeddings (already being generated) for semantic matching\n- Per-user pulse configuration: topics, keywords, preferred categories\n- API: `GET /api/v1/pulses/:id/stories` returns curated story list\n\n**6b. ShowPrep / PrepOS**\n- Show preparation interface: editors curate a story list for an upcoming broadcast\n- Rundown model: ordered list of stories with notes, time allocations, talking points\n- AI-generated talking points per story using FirstDraft (Phase 2)\n- Print/export view for production staff\n\n**6d.
